Q1	SELECT title.production_year, title.id  FROM title ORDER BY title.id ASC, title.season_nr ASC   LIMIT 100
Q2	SELECT aka_title.production_year, aka_title.kind_id, aka_title.episode_of_id  FROM aka_title ORDER BY aka_title.season_nr DESC   LIMIT 100
Q3	SELECT movie_info.id, movie_info.info_type_id, movie_info.movie_id  FROM movie_info  WHERE movie_info.movie_id >= 2310505 AND movie_info.info_type_id > 97 AND movie_info.id <= 7686186 ORDER BY movie_info.movie_id ASC, movie_info.info_type_id ASC   LIMIT 100
Q4	SELECT movie_companies.id, movie_companies.company_type_id  FROM movie_companies  WHERE movie_companies.company_id > 46 AND movie_companies.company_type_id = 2 AND movie_companies.id > 1409729 ORDER BY movie_companies.company_id ASC, movie_companies.company_type_id ASC   LIMIT 100
Q5	SELECT sum(distinct(title.kind_id)) AS c_10  FROM kind_type LEFT OUTER JOIN title ON kind_type.id = title.id GROUP BY title.id, title.imdb_id   LIMIT 100
Q6	SELECT aka_title.id  FROM aka_title  WHERE aka_title.id < 24595 AND aka_title.production_year = 2002 ORDER BY aka_title.id ASC, aka_title.production_year ASC   LIMIT 100
Q7	SELECT movie_keyword.movie_id, keyword.id, movie_keyword.keyword_id  FROM movie_keyword JOIN keyword ON movie_keyword.movie_id = keyword.id   LIMIT 100
Q8	SELECT aka_title.episode_of_id  FROM aka_title  WHERE aka_title.id < 264008 AND aka_title.kind_id >= 1 AND aka_title.production_year = 1970 ORDER BY aka_title.id ASC, aka_title.production_year ASC   LIMIT 100
Q9	SELECT sum(distinct(title.imdb_id)) AS c_10  FROM title GROUP BY title.kind_id   LIMIT 100
Q10	SELECT movie_info_idx.movie_id  FROM movie_info_idx  WHERE movie_info_idx.movie_id <= 1775180 GROUP BY movie_info_idx.movie_id   LIMIT 100
Q11	SELECT sum(title.imdb_id) AS c_10, avg(distinct(title.production_year)) AS c_11, title.episode_of_id  FROM title GROUP BY title.episode_of_id, title.season_nr   LIMIT 100
Q12	SELECT cast_info.person_id, char_name.id, cast_info.id AS id_1  FROM cast_info JOIN char_name ON cast_info.person_role_id = char_name.id  WHERE cast_info.person_role_id < 36819 AND char_name.id <= 1376863 AND cast_info.nr_order < 22 ORDER BY cast_info.person_role_id ASC, char_name.id ASC, cast_info.nr_order ASC   LIMIT 100
Q13	SELECT movie_keyword.id, min(movie_keyword.movie_id) AS c_11, min(movie_keyword.keyword_id) AS c_12  FROM movie_keyword GROUP BY movie_keyword.id   LIMIT 100
Q14	SELECT aka_title.production_year, aka_title.id  FROM aka_title LEFT OUTER JOIN title ON aka_title.movie_id = title.id   LIMIT 100
Q15	SELECT aka_name.person_id  FROM aka_name  WHERE aka_name.id = 586163 AND aka_name.person_id >= 84640 GROUP BY aka_name.id, aka_name.person_id   LIMIT 100
Q16	SELECT min(title.production_year) AS c_10, count(title.kind_id) AS c_11  FROM title  WHERE title.kind_id > 4 OR title.episode_of_id = 1381096 GROUP BY title.episode_of_id   LIMIT 100
Q17	SELECT cast_info.person_id, cast_info.movie_id, cast_info.id  FROM cast_info  WHERE cast_info.movie_id < 568764 AND cast_info.role_id = 4 AND cast_info.nr_order >= 48 ORDER BY cast_info.movie_id ASC, cast_info.nr_order ASC   LIMIT 100
Q18	SELECT title.production_year, count(title.imdb_id) AS c_11, sum(distinct(title.kind_id)) AS c_12  FROM movie_link JOIN title ON movie_link.id = title.id GROUP BY title.production_year, title.id   LIMIT 100
Q19	SELECT title.episode_of_id, title.imdb_id, title.production_year  FROM title ORDER BY title.season_nr ASC   LIMIT 100
Q20	SELECT movie_companies.company_type_id, movie_companies.id, movie_companies.movie_id  FROM movie_companies ORDER BY movie_companies.company_id ASC, movie_companies.movie_id ASC   LIMIT 100
Q21	SELECT company_name.id, company_name.imdb_id  FROM company_name GROUP BY company_name.id, company_name.imdb_id   LIMIT 100
Q22	SELECT variance(distinct(title.season_nr)) AS c_10, avg(title.production_year) AS c_11, title.episode_of_id  FROM title GROUP BY title.episode_of_id, title.kind_id   LIMIT 100
Q23	SELECT person_info.info_type_id  FROM person_info  WHERE person_info.id > 1874207 AND person_info.info_type_id >= 38 AND person_info.person_id > 1284830 ORDER BY person_info.info_type_id ASC, person_info.person_id ASC, person_info.id DESC   LIMIT 100
Q24	SELECT min(distinct(movie_keyword.movie_id)) AS c_10, movie_keyword.id, movie_keyword.keyword_id  FROM movie_keyword GROUP BY movie_keyword.id, movie_keyword.keyword_id   LIMIT 100

Q29	SELECT title.episode_of_id, title.id  FROM movie_link LEFT OUTER JOIN title ON movie_link.id = title.id ORDER BY title.id ASC, title.season_nr ASC, movie_link.link_type_id ASC   LIMIT 100

Q35	SELECT title.kind_id, count(distinct(title.production_year)) AS c_11, variance(title.episode_nr) AS c_12  FROM kind_type LEFT OUTER JOIN title ON kind_type.id = title.id GROUP BY title.season_nr, title.kind_id   LIMIT 100
